Time stamp string length. The string format is \char`\"{}yy/\+M\+M/dd,hh\+:mm\+:ss+/-\/zz\char`\"{} (Year/\+Month/\+Day,Hour\+:\+Min\+:Seconds+/-\/\+Time\+Zone). One extra byte is added for the null character.

\index{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete}!le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Msg\+Ref\+\_\+t}}]{msg\+Ref}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{le__sms__interface_8h_aca1691010c88995cb47225f2889910fa}
Delete a Message data structure.

It deletes the Message data structure and all the allocated memory is freed. If several users own the Message object (e.\+g., several handler functions registered for S\+M\+S message reception), the Message object will only be deleted if one User owns the Message object.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the caller is passing a bad pointer into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em msg\+Ref} & Reference to the message object. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{le__sms__interface_8h_aff755186b683b94ba2788b48e28284a3}{}\index{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete\+From\+Storage@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete\+From\+Storage}}
\index{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete\+From\+Storage@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete\+From\+Storage}!le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete\+From\+Storage}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Delete\+From\+Storage (

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{le__sms__interface_8h_aff755186b683b94ba2788b48e28284a3}
Delete an S\+M\+S message from the storage area.

Verifies first if the parameter is valid, then it checks the modem state can support message deleting.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+L\+T Function failed to perform the deletion. 

L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+M\+E\+M\+O\+R\+Y Message storage is not available. 

L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+K Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the caller is passing a bad pointer into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em msg\+Ref} & Reference to the message object. \\

\end{DoxyParams}

Get the binary Message.

Output parameters are updated with the binary message content and the length of the raw binary message in bytes. If the binary data exceed the value of \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} input parameter, a L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W error code is returned and \textquotesingle{}raw\textquotesingle{} is filled until \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} bytes.

L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W Message length exceed the maximum length. 

L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+K Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyReturn}

If the Telephone number string exceeds the value of \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} parameter, L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W error code is returned and \textquotesingle{}tel\textquotesingle{} is filled until \textquotesingle{}len-\/1\textquotesingle{} characters and a null-\/character is implicitly appended at the end of \textquotesingle{}tel\textquotesingle{}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+L\+T Service is not available.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+O\+W Telephone number length exceed the maximum length.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+K Function succeeded. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If telephone destination number is too long is too long (max L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+D\+M\+D\+E\+F\+S\+\_\+\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return.

Set the Telephone destination number.

Telephone number is defined in I\+T\+U-\/\+T recommendations E.\+164/\+E.163. E.\+164 numbers can have a maximum of fifteen digits and are usually written with a \textquotesingle{}+\textquotesingle{} prefix.
